*************** CZ low plus CE ***************

* This file contains:
**** CZ Airspace Files BELOW FL95 valid from effective date
**** Airspace of the czech neighbours (warning: this part is not updated on regular basis, users should check the situation before the flight at local authorities)
**** Dropzones: users should avoid entering dropzones without coordination with ATZ


****** (c) 2025 Jan Zahradka ******
******* Last update 01APR25 *******
******** EFFECTIVE 01APR25 ********


* This file was created on behalf of Aeroklub Ceske Republiky, it is free to use.
* It's optimised for Gliding and provides info for avoiding unintentional incidents
* The usage of this file is free of charge
* Freely share this for any kind of general aviation purposes including commercial devices such as planning tools, IGC loggers, navigation devices ect.
* Updates are released on regular basis on page https://www.aeroklub.cz/vzdusny-prostor/

*********************************************
***** LKAA DROPZONES (Dangerous Areas) ******

* This section contains areas around airfields with parachute markings.
* There are two sizes of dropzones: 3 NM for whole-week dropzones (Pribram, Most, Klatovy, Prostejov) and 2 NM for irregular para operations.
* It is not a part of the official LKAA definition however it is recommended to acknowledge these areas during gliding.
* Users should avoid entering Dropzones without coordination with ATZ
* Competitions: coordinate each competition day, only inoperative dropzones should be marked as inactive airspace for the task.

*Setting colour and line of Danger (Q) airspace
AC Q
SP 0,2,127,0,127
SB -1,-1,-1


****** empty template for dropzone ******
*AC Q
*AN DROPZONE
*AF
*AH FL 95
*AL 0 AGL
*V X=
*DC 2 *NM
